# Enemy Sprite Generation Prompts — Full Database

All ~400 unique RO Classic monsters, sorted by body type. Each prompt is in a code block for easy copying.

**Body Type Rules:**
- **Humanoid/Biped** (2 legs + 2 arms + head): Uses `true T-pose`, `legs straight and slightly apart`
- **Quadruped** (4 legs): Uses `standing on 4 legs`
- **Blob/Slime** (round, no limbs): Uses `no arms, no legs, no appendages`
- **Other types**: Adapted per body shape

---

## Blob / Slime

### angeling
```text
solo, chibi style, full body, simple round blob, no arms, no legs, no appendages, no limbs, floating gently in the air, front view, directly facing camera, centered composition, plain white background, simple background,

angelic poring creature, pure white translucent jelly blob body, perfectly round bouncy slime form, glossy pearlescent surface with pearlescent white highlights,

big expressive shiny blue eyes with white highlights, happy serene smiling curved mouth, small cute pink blush cheeks, golden angel halo floating above head, small white feathered angel wings sprouting from sides of round body,

no flames, no fire, no smoke, no particles, no aura, no glowing effects, no special effects,
high detail sprite, painted anime style, soft cel shading, vibrant colors, clean lines, masterpiece, best quality, absurdres, very detailed jelly texture, glossy reflections, heavenly golden glow, sharp focus
```
